—Å—Å—ã–ª–∫–∞
11:19 
def flatter(li):
    li_flattened = []
    for el in li:
        if isinstance(el, list):
            el_flattened = flatter(el)
            li_flattened.extend(el_flattened)
        else:
            li_flattened.append(el)
    return li_flattened

myli = [1, 2, 3, [3, [6, 3]], 6]
myliflattened = flatter(myli)
print(myliflattened)
